## 1. Executive Summary
**Executive Summary**

This week's scan of 613 affiliate opportunities yielded no immediate action items, with zero products qualifying for Tier 1 or Tier 2 review status. Eight products advanced to Tier 3 evergreen monitoring, including Facebook Ads Blackbook and several AI-powered tools spanning health, social media, and content creation verticals. The market remains heavily saturated with AI/SaaS launches (82 products), while our watchlist expanded to eight prospects requiring continued observation, suggesting a cooling period in high-priority launch activity.

## 2. Market Overview
**Market Overview**

This week's scan of 613 products revealed a market dominated by AI and SaaS launches, with 82 products in the primary AI/SaaS launch category representing the strongest segment. No products reached Tier 1 or 2 priority levels, indicating a week of incremental rather than breakthrough launches. The evergreen Tier 3 portfolio shows diversification across Facebook advertising, video marketing, automation tools, and AI-powered health solutions. Our watchlist reflects continued AI tool proliferation with 8 products under monitoring, while 511 products (83%) were filtered out as non-viable. The category distribution confirms AI/SaaS dominance with 97 total products across AI-related segments, signaling sustained but potentially oversaturated market activity in this vertical.
